[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:161[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m175[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:    [0m[39mdatao = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:    [0m[39mdatao += exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:165[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m176[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->offset, buf_size, [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:    [0m[39mdatao = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m173[0m[39m:    [0m[39mn->order = EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:    [0m[39mdatao += exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao, buf_size, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/exif-data.[0m[1;92mc:192[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m200[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mdoff = exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39md + offset + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, data->priv->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:    [0m[39melse[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mdoff = offset + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Sanity checks *[0m[35m/[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_log [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->priv->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_DEBUG, [0m[32m"ExifData"[0m[39m,[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"Tag starts past end of buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, doff, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Core Issue & Root Cause[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function exif_get_slong [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcalled via exif_get_long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unconditionally reads [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfour bytes from a buffer pointer without ensuring that those bytes lie within the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated region.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In exif_mnote_data_fuji_load, the call at line [0m[1;36m175[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        datao += [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     lacks a preceding bounds check guaranteeing at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes are readable at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`buf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m`. Although an earlier CHECKOVERFLOW on `n->offset` covers the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial datao calculation, it does *not* protect the *dynamic* offset used here [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mafter adding the maker‐note pointer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so malformed inputs can make `datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed buf_size and trigger a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read past the end.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.c[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Function: exif_mnote_data_fuji_load[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Insert a CHECKOVERFLOW on the dynamic offset just before invoking [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_get_long for the maker-note pointer.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Strategy[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Immediately before line [0m[1;36m175[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe call to exif_get_long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Ensure we have room for a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte pointer at buf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao, buf_size, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39men->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataFuji"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Then perform:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      datao += [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, EXIF_BYTE_ORDER_INTEL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Leave the subsequent two‐byte CHECKOVERFLOW [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m176[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in place, as it guards[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlater parsing.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Logic & Safety[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors the guard in exif_data_load_data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich ensures `offset [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m <= size` before calling exif_get_long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without altering any downstream [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing logic.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Good data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwell-formed Fuji maker-notes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will still satisfy the new check and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollow the same code path.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Malformed or truncated data will now be caught safely, logged as “Short [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMakerNote,” and return early, preventing the heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. No Other Code Changes[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - exif-utils.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexif_get_slong, exif_get_long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains untouched.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to the fuzzer harness or test suite—these are explicitly forbidden [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand unnecessary.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing CHECKOVERFLOW macro is reused, avoiding new utility functions or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmacros.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This check only rejects pathological inputs that would have previously overrun[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe buffer; it does not alter any valid parsing.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging and return behavior on corruption remains consistent with existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“Short MakerNote” paths.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance impact on well-formed metadata due to a single integer addition[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand comparison.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Validation[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild libexif and rerun exif_from_data_fuzzer. The previously crashing input[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould now be logged and handled gracefully without ASan errors.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing unit tests and fuzzing harness remain green.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m300[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi >= n->count[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return NULL;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m301[0m[39m:        return mnote_fuji_tag_get_title [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.tag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m302[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m303[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m304[0m[39m:static const char *[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m305:e[0m[39mxif_mnote_data_fuji_get_description [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *d, unsigned int i[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m306[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m307[0m[39m:    [0m[39mExifMnoteDataFuji *n = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteDataFuji *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m d;[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m311[0m[39m:        return mnote_fuji_tag_get_description [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.tag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m312[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m317[0m[39m:    [0m[39mExifByteOrder o_orig;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m318[0m[39m:    [0m[39mExifMnoteDataFuji *n = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteDataFuji *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m d;[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m320[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m321[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!n[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m:    [0m[39mn->order = o;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m327[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mcontinue;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m328[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.order = o;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m329[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mexif_array_set_byte_order [0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.format, [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.data,[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m330[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mn->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.components, o_orig, o[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.[0m[1;92mc:1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m40[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m:#include <stdlib.h>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m:#include <string.h>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m:#include <config.h>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m:#include <libexif/exif-byte-order.h>[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m:#include <libexif/exif-utils.h>[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m:#include [0m[32m"exif-mnote-data-fuji.h"[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m:#define [0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset,datasize,structsize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m offset >= datasize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mstructsize > datasize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset > datasize - structsize [0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m:struct _MNoteFujiDataPrivate [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m:     [0m[39mExifByteOrder order;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:static void[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m38:e[0m[39mxif_mnote_data_fuji_clear [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteDataFuji *n[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:     [0m[39mExifMnoteData *d = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifMnoteData *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m n;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root-Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   After reviewing the bounds checks and offset arithmetic in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif-mnote-data-fuji.c, the fundamental error is that the Fuji “load” routine [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-counts the [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m-byte TIFF header slice.  In the overarching EXIF loader [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mexif_data_load_data_content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, libexif strips off the first [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes of the EXIF [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader and passes  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • buf → start of TIFF data  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • buf_size → total TIFF bytes  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • offset → IFD0’s pointer into “buf”  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   directly into exif_mnote_data_fuji_load.  However, the FUJI code then [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally does  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     datao = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   effectively jumping [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes past the correct start, so all subsequent reads use [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmisaligned pointers.  This misalignment allows the read at buf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to fall just outside the buffer without triggering the existing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds check.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Patch Steps  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Remove the extra “+ [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m” in the initial offset calculation.  Change:  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       datao = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       datao = n->offset;  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Update the very first CHECKOVERFLOW to reflect the correct struct size [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  Change:  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->offset, buf_size, [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to something like:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mn->offset, buf_size, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     thus ensuring there are at least [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m producer bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m for tag header + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe pointer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m available at buf + offset.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Immediately before calling [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + datao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add a precise [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds check on that read:  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, buf_size, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m log error; return; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This tightens verification exactly around the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Fix the data-entry pointer arithmetic inside the tag-loop.  Replace:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       dataofs = [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + dataofs, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset;  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with:  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       dataofs = [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + dataofs, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + n->offset;  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     so that larger data blocks are copied from the true MakerNote buffer base, not[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset by an extra [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m bytes.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   E. Audit and adjust any further “[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + n->offset” occurrences in this function, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring that every pointer into “buf” correctly uses n->offset as the sole base.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We leave all fuzzy-harness code, utility functions, and test suites untouched.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – We do not modify CHECKOVERFLOW’s definition, only how callers use it.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – All other loops and tag-parsing logic remain the same; only pointer arithmetic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand associated bounds checks change.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Fix Works  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • By removing the spurious “+[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m,” datao now points exactly at the IFD0 offset [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the TIFF buffer passed to the FUJI loader.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • The revised CHECKOVERFLOW parameters align properly with the [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many subsequent [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m-byte reads, catching all cases where the fuzzer might craft a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtoo-small buffer.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   • The same pattern of bounds checks is retained for all further loops [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mshort-reads, tag headers, component data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so no new vulnerabilities are [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduced.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – There is no change to public APIs or the layout of MakerNote entries; only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal indexing is corrected.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – If any downstream code assumed FUJI loader implicitly skipped [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m header bytes, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat expectation is incorrect—the actual TIFF loader already removed them.  This [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch restores correct behavior.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Smoke-test with known good EXIF files and run the existing fuzz harness to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure no regressions.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference in Codebase  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The IFD0 processing in exif-data.c strips a [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m-byte header before invoking [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mload.  Parallel logic in Nikon/Sony modules does _not_ re-add those bytes, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirming Fuji’s “+[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m” was anomalous.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImplementation Outline:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– In libexif/fuji/exif-mnote-data-fuji.c, inside exif_mnote_data_fuji_load:  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Change the first CHECKOVERFLOW to use [0m[33mstructSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m+[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Change datao assignment to datao = n->offset  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Insert [0m[1;35mCHECKOVERFLOW[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdatao+[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, buf_size, [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before exif_get_long  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Adjust dataofs arithmetic in the tag-parsing loop by removing “+[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m”  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
